name:L‚Äça‚Äçi‚Äçj‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçx‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçc‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçs‚Äçh‚Äçu‚Äçb‚Äça
info:Superior Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Friends
info:17 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted March 11, 2024
msg:Location: Next to the entrance to the North Square of Wuxi Station, it takes 2 minutes to walk from the hotel to the station. It's not noisy when facing north, but the view of the construction site is better. Last time, I preferred facing south where I could see the train and Sanyang Plaza skyline.

Public area: The escalator is not working, which makes it a little troublesome to get from the train station/subway to the lobby. However, the size and decoration of the public area are very comfortable. The minivan in the lobby bar is very cute and the elevator is fast enough.

Room: The area is large, and many sofas and chairs are very comfortable. However, the use of large glass in the bathroom of the twin room is a bit hard to say. Without a smart toilet/wireless charging/smart TV, it feels a little different from the new hotels after 2020. The small refrigerator does not have power, which is not very pleasant.

Breakfast: I feel that the breakfast during holidays is better than other chains at the same price. There are four freshly made flour wonton stalls + pancake stalls + freshly made ramen stalls + hot and sour tofu soup stalls. The ramen and egg rolls are delicious, and the fruit and bread stations are also of very high quality. The only drawback is that there are no cold milk coffee options.

Service: Our hotel seems to be the crew hotel of the four major Hunan airlines including Geely, Ruili, Xiangpeng, so there is always an endless stream of crew members in the lobby. Ctrip's order was also recognized by the front desk (I remember that I didn't stay for a few nights) and the membership also gave me a drink coupon for the lobby bar, which was a surprise. If you want ice at night, it will be delivered to the door in 5 minutes. However, I still hope that Holiday Inn can provide smart TVs/free laundry/robot delivery like domestic chains, so that ordering takeout can reduce the ideological struggle when I go to the room in the middle of the night and find that the room ordering menu is gone.
----------------------------------------
